# Feiten daily pulse
feiten_daily_pulse = {
	potential = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_daily_pulse }
	}
	
	on_activation = {
		set_province_flag = feiten_daily_pulse
		log = "Feiten daily pulse triggered [GetDate]:" # Disable this before adding to main build to reduce log spam
		Y20 = {
			feiten_update_shuimu_capacity = yes
			feiten_update_firestorm_experimental = yes
			feiten_update_stasis_experimental = yes
			update_artifice_points = yes
			feiten_update_skyport_balance = yes
			feiten_update_skypost_duty = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_institution = enlightenment
					has_country_flag = feiten_next_institution_enlightenment
				}
				remove_country_modifier = feiten_university_row
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_institution = industrialization
					has_country_flag = feiten_next_institution_industrialization
				}
				remove_country_modifier = feiten_university_row
			}
		}
	}

	
	on_deactivation = {
		clr_province_flag = feiten_daily_pulse
		log = "Feiten daily pulse triggered [GetDate]:" # Disable this before adding to main build to reduce log spam
		Y20 = {
			feiten_update_shuimu_capacity = yes
			feiten_update_firestorm_experimental = yes
			feiten_update_stasis_experimental = yes
			update_artifice_points = yes
			feiten_update_skyport_balance = yes
			feiten_update_skypost_duty = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_institution = enlightenment
					has_country_flag = feiten_next_institution_enlightenment
				}
				remove_country_modifier = feiten_university_row
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_institution = industrialization
					has_country_flag = feiten_next_institution_industrialization
				}
				remove_country_modifier = feiten_university_row
			}
		}
	}
}

# on_monthly
feiten_monthly_pulse = {
	potential = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				is_month = 0
				NOT = { is_month = 1 }
			}
			AND = {
				is_month = 2
				NOT = { is_month = 3 }
			}
			AND = {
				is_month = 4
				NOT = { is_month = 5 }
			}
			AND = {
				is_month = 6
				NOT = { is_month = 7 }
			}
			AND = {
				is_month = 8
				NOT = { is_month = 9 }
			}
			AND = {
				is_month = 10
				NOT = { is_month = 11 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	on_activation = {
		Y20 = {
			# Monthly Skypost duties
            if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = feitenSkypostDutyEff value = 100 } }

# Feiten island colonization modifier
feiten_island_colonization_handler = {
	potential = { Y20 = { exists = yes } }

	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		owned_by = Y20
		is_city = no
	}
	
	#Province scope
	on_activation = {
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = feiten_island_colonization_mod
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	
	on_deactivation = {
		remove_province_modifier = feiten_island_colonization_mod
		if = {
			limit = {
				owned_by = Y20
				is_city = yes
			}
			remove_province_triggered_modifier = feiten_island_colonization_handler
			add_base_production = 1
		}
	}
}

# Feiten skyport handler thingy
feiten_skyport_handler_mod = {
	potential = { Y20 = { exists = yes } }

	trigger = { owner = { NOT = { war_with = Y20 } } }

	trade_value = 1
	province_trade_power_value = 5
	
	#Province scope
	on_activation = {
		Y20 = {
			change_variable = {
				which = feitenActiveSkyports
				value = 1
			}
		}
		remove_trade_modifier = {
			who = Y20
			key = "Feiten Skyport"
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = feitenActiveSkyports
					value = 20
				}
			}
			add_trade_modifier = {
				who = Y20
				duration = -1
				power = 50
				key = "Feiten Skyport"
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = feitenActiveSkyports
					value = 15
				}
			}
			add_trade_modifier = {
				who = Y20
				duration = -1
				power = 45
				key = "Feiten Skyport"
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = feitenActiveSkyports
					value = 10
				}
			}
			add_trade_modifier = {
				who = Y20
				duration = -1
				power = 35
				key = "Feiten Skyport"
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = feitenActiveSkyports
					value = 5
				}
			}
			add_trade_modifier = {
				who = Y20
				duration = -1
				power = 25
				key = "Feiten Skyport"
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_trade_modifier = {
				who = Y20
				duration = -1
				power = 15
				key = "Feiten Skyport"
			}
		}
	}
	
	on_deactivation = {
		remove_trade_modifier = {
			who = Y20
			key = "Feiten Skyport"
		}
		remove_province_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_open_door
		remove_province_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_trade_protectionism
		remove_province_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_air_garrison
		Y20 = {
			subtract_variable = {
				which = feitenActiveSkyports
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
}
